					<p class="qodef-m-text" style="margin-top: 20px">Located in the Sultanahmet district of Istanbul’s historic peninsula, just off the Little Hagia Sophia Mosque, Aya Garden Cafe &amp; Restaurant is one of Istanbul’s most popular venues, offering guests both delicious cuisine and a peaceful atmosphere. The wide range of dishes offered, from traditional Turkish cuisine to examples of international cuisine, are prepared with fresh ingredients. There are a variety of options for breakfast, lunch, and dinner. Special menu options are also available for special occasions and events.</p>

<script>
(function(){
  var fab = document.getElementById('socialFab');
  var toggle = document.getElementById('socialFabToggle');
  if(!fab || !toggle) return;

  // Varsayılan açık
  fab.classList.add('is-open');
  toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded','true');

  toggle.addEventListener('click', function(){
    var isOpen = fab.classList.toggle('is-open');
    toggle.setAttribute('aria-expanded', isOpen ? 'true' : 'false');
    toggle.setAttribute('aria-label', isOpen ? 'Sosyal bağlantıları gizle' : 'Sosyal bağlantıları göster');
  });
})();

					const lazyloadBackgrounds = document.querySelectorAll( `.e-con.e-parent:not(.e-lazyloaded)` );
					const lazyloadBackgroundObserver = new IntersectionObserver( ( entries ) => {
						entries.forEach( ( entry ) => {
							if ( entry.isIntersecting ) {
								let lazyloadBackground = entry.target;
								if( lazyloadBackground ) {
									lazyloadBackground.classList.add( 'e-lazyloaded' );
								}
								lazyloadBackgroundObserver.unobserve( entry.target );
							}
						});

					lazyloadBackgrounds.forEach( ( lazyloadBackground ) => {
						lazyloadBackgroundObserver.observe( lazyloadBackground );
					} );
				};
				const events = [
					'DOMContentLoaded',
					'elementor/lazyload/observe',
				];

<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function(){
  document.querySelectorAll('#qodef-page-header .widget.widget_polylang .pll-switcher-select').forEach(function(sel){
    if (sel.dataset.enhanced === '1') return;
    sel.dataset.enhanced = '1';

    // Kapsayıcı + elemanlar
    var dd = document.createElement('div'); dd.className = 'lang-dd';
    var btn = document.createElement('button'); btn.type = 'button'; btn.className = 'lang-dd__btn';
    var list = document.createElement('div'); list.className = 'lang-dd__list';

    // Yerleştir
    var parent = sel.parentNode;
    parent.appendChild(dd);
    dd.appendChild(btn);
    dd.appendChild(list);

    // Seçenekler
    var opts = Array.from(sel.options);
    var current = opts.find(o => o.selected) || opts[0];

    function codeOf(opt){
      try { return (JSON.parse(opt.dataset.lang).slug || opt.text).toUpperCase(); }
      catch(e){ return (opt.text || '').slice(0,2).toUpperCase(); }
    }

    function renderBtn(){
      btn.innerHTML = '<span class="lang-badge">'+ codeOf(current) +'</span><span>'+ current.text +'</span>';
    }

    function renderList(){
      list.innerHTML = '';
      opts.forEach(function(o){
        var a = document.createElement('a');
        a.href = o.value;
        a.className = 'lang-dd__item';
        a.innerHTML = '<span class="lang-badge">'+ codeOf(o) +'</span><span>'+ o.text +'</span>';
        list.appendChild(a);
      });
    }

    renderBtn(); renderList();

    // --- Hover kontrolü: gecikmeli kapanma ---
    var hideTimer = null;

    dd.addEventListener('mouseenter', function(){
      if (hideTimer) { clearTimeout(hideTimer); hideTimer = null; }
      dd.classList.add('open');   // CSS ile birlikte çalışır
    });

    dd.addEventListener('mouseleave', function(){
      hideTimer = setTimeout(function(){
        dd.classList.remove('open');
      }, 180); // hızlı geçişlerde kapanmayı geciktir
    });

    // Güvenlik: sayfada bir yere tıklanınca kapat (hover dışına çıkıldıysa)
    document.addEventListener('click', function(){
      dd.classList.remove('open');
    });

    // Edge case: select değişirse yönlendir
    sel.addEventListener('change', function(){ location.href = sel.value; });
  });
});




(function($){
  function buildCustomMobileLang(){
    var $mobileInner = $('#qodef-page-mobile-header-inner');
    if(!$mobileInner.length) return;

    // Varsa tekrar oluşturma
    if($('#pll-mobile-dd').length) return;

    // Kaynak: sayfadaki ilk Polylang widget'ı
    var $src = $('.widget.widget_polylang .pll-switcher-select').first();
    if(!$src.length) return;

    // Mevcut dili al
    var currentText = $src.find('option:selected').text();
    var currentLang = (document.documentElement.lang || '').toLowerCase().indexOf('tr')===0 ? 'TR' : 'EN';

    // Custom dropdown HTML
    var $wrap = $(`
      <div id="pll-mobile-dd" class="pll-dd" aria-expanded="false">
        <button type="button" class="pll-dd__btn">
          <span class="pll-dd__badge">${currentLang}</span>
          <span class="pll-dd__label">${currentText}</span>
          <span class="pll-dd__chev"></span>
        </button>
        <div class="pll-dd__list" hidden></div>
      </div>
    `);

    // Liste elemanlarını ekle
    $src.find('option').each(function(){
      var txt = $(this).text();
      var url = $(this).attr('data-href') || $(this).data('href') || $(this).val();
      var $item = $(`<div class="pll-dd__item">${txt}</div>`);
      $item.attr('data-url', url);
      if(txt === currentText) $item.addClass('is-active');
      $wrap.find('.pll-dd__list').append($item);
    });

    // Hamburgerden önce ekle
    var $opener = $mobileInner.find('.qodef-mobile-header-opener').last();
    if($opener.length){
      $wrap.insertBefore($opener);
    }else{
      $mobileInner.append($wrap);
    }

    // Olaylar
    $wrap.on('click', '.pll-dd__btn', function(e){
      e.stopPropagation();
      var open = $wrap.attr('aria-expanded')==='true';
      $('.pll-dd').attr('aria-expanded','false').find('.pll-dd__list').prop('hidden', true);
      $wrap.attr('aria-expanded', !open);
      $wrap.find('.pll-dd__list').prop('hidden', open);
    });

    $wrap.on('click', '.pll-dd__item', function(){
      var url = $(this).data('url');
      if(url) window.location.href = url;
    });

    $(document).on('click', function(){
      $wrap.attr('aria-expanded','false');
      $wrap.find('.pll-dd__list').prop('hidden', true);
    });
  }

  $(window).on('load', function(){
    buildCustomMobileLang();
  });
})(jQuery);






(function(){
  function wrapOnce(img){
    if (!img || img.closest('a')) return;

    const item   = img.closest('.qodef-m-item');
    const titleN = item && item.querySelector('.qodef-e-heading-title');
    const title  = (img.getAttribute('alt') || (titleN ? titleN.textContent.trim() : '') || 'Photo');

    const a = document.createElement('a');
    a.href = img.currentSrc || img.src;               // sadece bu görüntü
    a.className = 'lb-on';
    a.setAttribute('data-elementor-open-lightbox','yes');
    a.setAttribute('data-elementor-lightbox-title', title);
    // DİKKAT: slideshow/grup vermiyoruz → sadece tıklanan resim açılır

    img.parentNode.insertBefore(a, img);
    a.appendChild(img);
  }

  function init(){
    document.querySelectorAll('.qodef-qi-pricing-list .qodef-e-image img').forEach(wrapOnce);
  }

  // İlk yüklemede
  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', init);
  } else { init(); }

  // Elementor editörde/yeniden render’da
  if (window.elementorFrontend && elementorFrontend.hooks) {
    elementorFrontend.hooks.addAction('frontend/element_ready/global', init);
  }

  // Sonradan gelen elemanlar için emniyet (lazy/repeater)
  const mo = new MutationObserver(() => init());
  mo.observe(document.documentElement, {childList:true, subtree:true});
})();



</script>

</html>
